cT-ALL gene signatures to predict relapse and outcome Peyronlab

Network presentation

Here we present 5 PPI networks that were used to identify a relapse gene-signature in cT-ALL:

  • Hunet: The probabilistic functional gene network Hunet v1 (http://www.functionalnet.org/).
  • StringDB: Homo sapiens protein links v11 from the String database (https://string-db.org)
  • Biogrid: Multi validated physical interaction v3.5 from the Biogrid database from the GeneMANIA archives (http://genemania.org)
  • RegNetwork: Human regulatory relationships network from RegNetwork (http://regnetworkweb.org)
  • Kinome: Human kinases interactions partners from AP-MS analysis (https://sec-explorer.shinyapps.io/Kinome_interactions/)

Each network is presented under two forms, the complete and pruned datasets.

Network data can be downloaded for each network as .rds files at

https://github.com/Peyronlab/Peyronlab.github.io/

To start:

Select a network in the top navigation bar.

Signatures detailed information

Reproducibility OS ,Reproducibility Rel.:

  • Score from 0 to 3 indicating the number of cohorts on which the signature significantly predicts either overall survival or relapse.

Reproducibility qPCR:

  • Score from 0 to 1 indicating the ability of the signature to predict relapse, or not.
  • NA is for signatures that were not tested.

Symbol formula:

  • Formula to compute patient scores using expression of given genes.

Dirgenerank parameters:

  • ex: describes the initializing vector of weight (either coxph coefficients or 0)
  • d: describes the balance parameter between W and ex.
Cite:

Raphaël Bonnet 1, 2, Roger Rezzonico 3, Véronique Imbert 1, 2, Chloé Arfeuille 4, Julien Fassy 5, Bernard Mari 5, Frédéric Reinier 1,2, Aurélie Caye4, Hélène Cavé 4, Sofie Degerman 6,7, Marc Mansour 8, Anthony Moorman 9, Pieter Van Vlierberghe 10, Pierre-Simon Rohrlich 1, 2, 11, Jean-François Peyron 1, 2
